Introduction

Base URL: http://localhost:8000

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Authenticating requests

This API is not authenticated.

AppointmentRace

–ú–µ—Ç–æ–¥—ã –æ—Ç–≤–µ—á–∞—é—â–∏–µ –∑–∞ –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å—å —É—á–∞—Å—Ç–Ω–∏–∫–æ–≤

Toggle

requires authentication

–ó–∞–ø–∏—Å–∞—Ç—å—Å—è –∏ –æ—Ç–º–µ–Ω–∏—Ç—å –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å—å –Ω–∞ –≥–æ–Ω–∫—É

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost:8000/api/races/24/toggle-appointment-race" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"surname\": \"explicabo\",
    \"patronymic\": \"quaerat\",
    \"dateOfBirth\": \"2025-04-22T11:34:52\",
    \"city\": \"ullam\",
    \"region\": \"quo\",
    \"inn\": \"voluptas\",
    \"snils\": \"quia\",
    \"phoneNumber\": \"eos\",
    \"startNumber\": 22,
    \"group\": \"hic\",
    \"rank\": \"animi\",
    \"rankNumber\": \"modi\",
    \"community\": \"facere\",
    \"coach\": \"qui\",
    \"motoStamp\": \"commodi\",
    \"locationId\": \"delectus\",
    \"gradeId\": \"aut\",
    \"numberAndSeria\": \"animi\",
    \"documentIds\": [
        18
    ],
    \"userId\": 5
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/races/24/toggle-appointment-race"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "surname": "explicabo",
    "patronymic": "quaerat",
    "dateOfBirth": "2025-04-22T11:34:52",
    "city": "ullam",
    "region": "quo",
    "inn": "voluptas",
    "snils": "quia",
    "phoneNumber": "eos",
    "startNumber": 22,
    "group": "hic",
    "rank": "animi",
    "rankNumber": "modi",
    "community": "facere",
    "coach": "qui",
    "motoStamp": "commodi",
    "locationId": "delectus",
    "gradeId": "aut",
    "numberAndSeria": "animi",
    "documentIds": [
        18
    ],
    "userId": 5
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

Example response (200):


{
    "status": "success",
    "message": "–ó–∞–ø–∏—Å—å –Ω–∞ –≥–æ–Ω–∫—É —É—Å–ø–µ—à–Ω–æ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∞."
}

Example response (404):


{
    "status": "error",
    "message": "–ó–∞–ø—Ä–∞—à–∏–≤–∞–µ–º—ã–π —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å –Ω–µ –Ω–∞–π–¥–µ–Ω."
}

Example response (404):


{
    "status": "error",
    "message": "messages.appointment.create.grade_not_exists"
}

Example response (409):

    "status": "error",
    "message": "messages.error.exists_appointment_race"
}

Example response (422):

    "message": "messages.appointment.create_table.many_documents",
    "documents": []

If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

POST api/races/{id}/toggle-appointment-race

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

URL Parameters

id   integer   

The ID of the race. Example: 24

Body Parameters

surname   string   

Example: explicabo

patronymic   string   

Example: quaerat

dateOfBirth   string   

–ó–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ø–æ–ª—è value –Ω–µ —è–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç—Å—è –¥–∞—Ç–æ–π. Example: 2025-04-22T11:34:52

city   string   

Example: ullam

region   string  optional  

Example: quo

inn   string   

Example: voluptas

snils   string   

Example: quia

phoneNumber   string   

Example: eos

startNumber   integer   

–ó–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ø–æ–ª—è value –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω–æ –±—ã—Ç—å –Ω–µ –º–µ–Ω—å—à–µ 1. –ó–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ø–æ–ª—è value –Ω–µ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å –±–æ–ª—å—à–µ 999. Example: 22

group   string   

Example: hic

rank   string   

Example: animi

rankNumber   string  optional  

Example: modi

community   string  optional  

Example: facere

coach   string  optional  

Example: qui

motoStamp   string   

Example: commodi

locationId   string   

The id of an existing record in the locations table. Example: delectus

gradeId   string   

The id of an existing record in the grades table. Example: aut

commandId   string  optional  

The id of an existing record in the commands table.

numberAndSeria   string   

Example: animi

documentIds   integer[]  optional  
userId   integer  optional  

The id of an existing record in the users table. Example: 5

curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/races/24/appointment-race/users" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"paginate\": false,
    \"page\": \"et\",
    \"limit\": 2
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/races/24/appointment-race/users"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "paginate": false,
    "page": "et",
    "limit": 2
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());

create

requires authentication

–°–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏–µ –≥–æ–Ω–∫–∏

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost:8000/api/races" \
    --header "Content-Type: multipart/form-data" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --form "name=qtbrspdhpfvzvczpaehycdjqcqpibewmyzeeaiyawtmyxtqrrpoxzmxtqrafkbidvyxljnnasekyzf"\
    --form "desc=dolorem"\
    --form "dateStart=2025-04-22T11:34:51"\
    --form "recordStart=2025-04-22T11:34:51"\
    --form "recordEnd=2025-04-22T11:34:51"\
    --form "trackId=4"\
    --form "gradeIds[]=2"\
    --form "locationId=quisquam"\
    --form "statusId=16"\
    --form "cupIds[]=16"\
    --form "images[]=@/tmp/php9s1d65" \
    --form "positionFile=@/tmp/phpQ03yiR" \
    --form "resultsFile=@/tmp/phpcA3ZxY" 
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/races"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "multipart/form-data",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

const body = new FormData();
body.append('name', 'qtbrspdhpfvzvczpaehycdjqcqpibewmyzeeaiyawtmyxtqrrpoxzmxtqrafkbidvyxljnnasekyzf');
body.append('desc', 'dolorem');
body.append('dateStart', '2025-04-22T11:34:51');
body.append('recordStart', '2025-04-22T11:34:51');
body.append('recordEnd', '2025-04-22T11:34:51');
body.append('trackId', '4');
body.append('gradeIds[]', '2');
body.append('locationId', 'quisquam');
body.append('statusId', '16');
body.append('cupIds[]', '16');
body.append('images[]', document.querySelector('input[name="images[]"]').files[0]);
body.append('positionFile', document.querySelector('input[name="positionFile"]').files[0]);
body.append('resultsFile', document.querySelector('input[name="resultsFile"]').files[0]);

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body,
}).then(response => response.json());

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost:8000/api/races/24/update" \
    --header "Content-Type: multipart/form-data" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --form "name=oktxrzqjgycagxssmnoegmdfcvwunqziarvvjkdbqdaxasnj"\
    --form "desc=odio"\
    --form "dateStart=2025-04-22T11:34:51"\
    --form "recordEnd=2025-04-22T11:34:51"\
    --form "recordStart=2025-04-22T11:34:51"\
    --form "trackId=4"\
    --form "imagesDel[]=ipsa"\
    --form "gradeIds[]=15"\
    --form "locationId=8"\
    --form "statusId=2"\
    --form "cupIds[]=12"\
    --form "imagesAdd[]=@/tmp/phpzATNUo" \
    --form "positionFile=@/tmp/php27Male" \
    --form "resultsFile=@/tmp/phpFzVFZ2" 
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/races/24/update"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "multipart/form-data",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

const body = new FormData();
body.append('name', 'oktxrzqjgycagxssmnoegmdfcvwunqziarvvjkdbqdaxasnj');
body.append('desc', 'odio');
body.append('dateStart', '2025-04-22T11:34:51');
body.append('recordEnd', '2025-04-22T11:34:51');
body.append('recordStart', '2025-04-22T11:34:51');
body.append('trackId', '4');
body.append('imagesDel[]', 'ipsa');
body.append('gradeIds[]', '15');
body.append('locationId', '8');
body.append('statusId', '2');
body.append('cupIds[]', '12');
body.append('imagesAdd[]', document.querySelector('input[name="imagesAdd[]"]').files[0]);
body.append('positionFile', document.querySelector('input[name="positionFile"]').files[0]);
body.append('resultsFile', document.querySelector('input[name="resultsFile"]').files[0]);

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body,
}).then(response => response.json());

    "http://localhost:8000/api/verification-email/verify" \

}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/verification-email/verify"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "code": 10
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
